              (function() {
                try {
                  var params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
                  var qTheme = params.get('theme');
                  var theme = (qTheme === 'dark' || qTheme === 'light') ? qTheme : localStorage.getItem('theme');
                  if (qTheme === 'dark' || qTheme === 'light') {
                    localStorage.setItem('theme', qTheme);
                    params.delete('theme');
                    var newUrl = params.size ? window.location.pathname + '?' + params : window.location.pathname;

                  }
                  if (theme === 'dark' || (!theme && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
                    document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
                  }
                } catch (e) {}

nedjeljama</h3><p class="text-foreground-muted text-sm lg:text-base leading-relaxed mb-3">Pitate se koje trgovine rade nedjeljom? Zato smo stvorili ovaj jednostavan alat koji vam pomaže brzo pronaći što je otvoreno u vašoj blizini.</p><p class="text-foreground-muted text-sm lg:text-base leading-relaxed mb-3">Naša baza podataka uključuje supermarkete, shopping centre, drogerije, trgovine elektronikom, trgovine namještajem i još mnogo toga u svim hrvatskim gradovima.</p><p class="text-foreground-muted text-sm lg:text-base
